0                                   1414      13.              COPY  SLISTMAC
                                    1415             =*******************************************************************
                                    1416             =*                                                                 *
                                    1417             =* Macros for the serialized manipulation of single linked lists   *
                                    1418             =* in memory.  These lists are of the PUSH/POP (LIFO) variety.     *
                                    1419             =* Serialization is achieved using the CDS and CS instructions.    *
                                    1420             =*                                                                 *
                                    1421             =*******************************************************************
0                                   1423             =*******************************************************************
                                    1424             =*                                                                 *
                                    1425             =* Single linked list head fields                                  *
                                    1426             =*                                                                 *
                                    1427             =*******************************************************************
                                    1428             =         MACRO
                                    1429             =&LAB     SHEAD
                                    1430             =         AIF   ('&LAB' EQ '').ERR
                                    1431             =&LAB     DS   0D                   Single linked CDS list
                                    1432             =&LAB.FP  DS    A                   Forward pointer
                                    1433             =&LAB.SEQ DS    A                   CDS sequence number
                                    1434             =         MEXIT
                                    1435             =.ERR     MNOTE 8,'Label (list name) required'
                                    1436             =         MEND
0                                   1438             =*******************************************************************
                                    1439             =*                                                                 *
                                    1440             =* Push an item onto a single linked list                          *
                                    1441             =*                                                                 *
                                    1442             =*******************************************************************
                                    1443             =         MACRO
                                    1444             =&LABEL   SPUSH &HEAD=,&ITEM=
                                    1445             =         LCLC  &X
                                    1446             =         AIF   ('&LABEL' EQ '').NOLAB
                                    1447             =&LABEL   LABEL ,
                                    1448             =.NOLAB   ANOP  ,
                                    1449             =         AIF   ('&HEAD' EQ '').ERR1
                                    1450             =         AIF   ('&ITEM' EQ '').ERR2
                                    1452             =         LM    R14,R15,&HEAD       Get fwd ptr and sequence number
                                    1453             =         LA    RVR,&ITEM           Point to new item
                                    1454             =         LOOP  BEGIN
                                    1455             =         LA    RS,1(R15)           Increment sequence
                                    1456             =         MVC   &ITEM.(L'&HEAD.FP),&HEAD.FP Set item fwd ptr
                                    1457             =         CDS   R14,RVR,&HEAD       Add item to list
                                    1458             =         UNTIL (Z),END
                                    1460             =         AGO   .EXIT
                                    1461             =.ERR1    MNOTE 8,'Head is a required parameter'
                                    1462             =         AGO   .EXIT
                                    1463             =.ERR2    MNOTE 8,'Item is a required parameter'
                                    1464             =.EXIT    ANOP  ,
                                    1465             =         MEND  ,
0                                   1467             =*******************************************************************
                                    1468             =*                                                                 *
                                    1469             =* Pop an item from a single linked list. Addr returned in RVR     *
1FILESERV (FILESE) (09:39) (22MAR04) FILESERV - Global data areas                                                           Page   10
0Current Usings:  (PZERO,R0)

0                                   1470             =* (zero if the list was empty).                                   *
                                    1471             =*                                                                 *
                                    1472             =*******************************************************************
                                    1473             =         MACRO
                                    1474             =&LABEL   SPOP  &HEAD=
                                    1475             =         AIF   ('&LABEL' EQ '').NOLAB
                                    1476             =&LABEL   LABEL ,
                                    1477             =.NOLAB   ANOP  ,
                                    1478             =         AIF   ('&HEAD' EQ '').ERR1
                                    1480             =         LM    RVR,RS,&HEAD        Get fwd and sequence number
                                    1481             =         LOOP  BEGIN
                                    1482             =         IF    (RVR,Z),EXIT        None to get
                                    1483             =         LR    R14,RVR             Point to first item
                                    1484             =         L     R14,0(R14)          Get fwd pointer
                                    1485             =         LA    R15,1(RS)           Increment sequence
                                    1486             =         CDS   RVR,R14,&HEAD       Remove item from list
                                    1487             =         UNTIL (Z),END
                                    1489             =         AGO   .EXIT
                                    1490             =.ERR1    MNOTE 8,'Head is a required parameter'
                                    1491             =.EXIT    ANOP  ,
                                    1492             =         MEND  ,

                                    1498             =*                                                                 *

0                                   8548     684.     *********************************************************************
                                    8549     685.     *  Open the datasets for an individual file system                  *
                                    8550     686.     *                                                                   *
                                    8551     687.     *   Input - @FSINIT                                                 *
                                    8552     688.     *             The FSB is allocated and cleared, but otherwise       *
                                    8553     689.     *           uninitialized.                                          *
                                    8554     690.     *             The parameter area is set up with the parameter type  *
                                    8555     691.     *           (string) and the proper keywords to retrieve the files  *
                                    8556     692.     *           for the file system in question.                        *
                                    8557     693.     *                                                                   *
                                    8558     694.     *  Output - FSB                                                     *
                                    8559     695.     *             If no files are found, then the total block count is  *
                                    8560     696.     *           zero, and the calling routine will take this as a       *
                                    8561     697.     *           signal to stop initializing FSBs                        *
                                    8562     698.     *                                                                   *
                                    8563     699.     *********************************************************************
